• Using cloudflare:cloudflare for Cloudflare deployment alignment and openai-docs for the OpenAI integration rules. I

  What I Found
  The directory is not currently a Git repo. It contains an existing static website under /C:/Users/Scott/Projects/
  AIFRED/website, an Android admin app under /C:/Users/Scott/Projects/AIFRED/android_admin, 52 beat catalog MP3s already
  inside /C:/Users/Scott/Projects/AIFRED/website/assets/audio/catalog, and the main product specs in the root.

  The docs lock the scope to three surfaces: one new Aifred VST3 plugin built from scratch, the existing website
  preserved and modernized, and the Android admin app preserved and modernized. The Halo spec defines the plugin’s core
  contract: raw audio metrics feed normalized domain scoring, then a single HaloState drives score, diagnosis, rings,
  fix list, compare mode, and assistant text. No UI panel should invent its own diagnosis.

  The images split cleanly into these groups:

  - Website assets: Website Asset..., website asset banner..., Brand Mascot Hero.jpg, and album art files.
  - Website look-and-feel references: Website LookANDFeel (1-3).jpg, showing the current dark/cyan mobile-first site
    direction, sticky header, catalog cards, and audio player.
  - Plugin/VST references: AIFREDVST concept Analysis mode.png, Reference Mode.png, Compare Mode.jpg, and Plugin
    Concept.jpg, showing the Halo meter, radar/fingerprint panel, session candles, fix list, dual compare rings, and
    neon diagnostic UI.
  - Admin references: AdminApp reference... plus Screenshot_...AIFR3D Admin 224 Beta.jpg, showing the Android control
    center with chat/upload/command tabs, server login, catalog/reference/website upload targeting, and live-site
    controls.
  - Unlabeled images are reference unless we explicitly map them as assets.

  Execution Plan

  1. Normalize the project layout before feature work. I will create a canonical monorepo shape that keeps the existing
     website and Android app intact while adding a fresh plugin area, likely apps/website, apps/android-admin, apps/
     plugin-aifred, packages/shared, infra/cloudflare, and docs. I will not force the website to match Cloudflare’s
     defaults. Cloudflare config will point to the real website files and preserve the website’s asset/catalog
     structure.
  2. Normalize filenames and routing. I will rename project-facing assets and catalog paths to Windows-safe, web-safe,
     relative names: lowercase, hyphenated, no spaces, no parentheses, no duplicate casing, and no hardcoded absolute
     paths. I will build a mapping file so references like Website Asset Brand.jpg become stable names such as website-
     asset-brand.jpg, and existing HTML/CSS/JS/catalog JSON references get updated together. For the beat catalog, I
     will preserve the fact that the MP3 files are already in the website files; I will only fix relative references and
     URL encoding as needed.
  3. Remove hardcoded paths and secrets. Anything like local /home/..., Windows user folders, absolute source paths, or
     embedded credentials will be moved to runtime config, .env examples, local properties, or Cloudflare secrets. The
     current Android Gradle file includes default admin credentials; that needs to be removed from distributable source
     and replaced with build-time or first-run configuration.
  4. Rework website routing around relative paths. The website should run locally on Windows by opening or serving the
     website folder and should deploy unchanged to Cloudflare. Asset references will stay relative, catalog entries will
     point to assets/audio/catalog/..., docs will point to assets/docs/..., and Cloudflare will be configured around
     that directory rather than forcing the site to relocate assets.
  5. Align Cloudflare to the checked-in website. I will add Cloudflare Pages/Workers configuration only after confirming
     the desired backend shape. The default plan is: static site from the website directory, API routes via Worker or
     Pages Functions, secrets via Cloudflare secrets, beat/audio/docs served from the deployed website assets, and any
     future storage only for things not already in the repo. If R2/D1/KV are needed, they will support uploads, sales,
     sessions, inquiries, or admin state, not replace the existing catalog files by default.
  6. Rebuild the Aifred plugin from scratch. I will scaffold a clean JUCE + CMake VST3 project rather than reusing old
     plugin code. The plugin implementation will follow the docs: audio feature extraction, domain normalization, Halo
     decision engine, presentation layer, three modes, reference profile ingestion, compare engine, diagnosis/fix
     templates, and immutable state snapshots between analysis and UI.
  7. Build the Halo state model first. Before drawing polish, I will define the shared types: AnalysisMode, Domain,
     Severity, Confidence, DomainAlignment, FixItem, and HaloState. Then I will implement scoring for tone, stereo,
     loudness, and dynamics using the weighting rules from the Halo and math specs. The UI will consume that state only.
  8. Build the plugin UI from the reference images. Analysis mode gets the single Halo, fingerprint/radar, value cards,
     settings; for Android they should be entered/admin-configured or provided through a secure backend route. The
     implementation should support both OpenAI and Ollama routing through a provider interface so either can be enabled
     without changing source code.
  11. Build distributable packages. For the plugin, that means a Windows VST3 build path and a distributable package/
     install/readme docs that explain where config lives without exposing secrets.
  12. Verify in phases. I will first validate asset routing and website load locally on Windows, then Cloudflare build/
     deploy behavior, then Android Gradle build, then plugin CMake/JUCE configuration, then VST3 packaging. For the
     website, I’ll verify the beat catalog uses the existing uploaded MP3 files rather than inventing new uploads.

      1 +#include "AnalysisEngine.h"
      2 +
      3 +#include <cmath>
      4 +#include <numbers>
      5 +
      6 +namespace aifred {
      7 +namespace {
      8 +
      9 +float safeSqrt(float value) {
     10 +  return std::sqrt(std::max(value, 0.0f));
     11 +}
     12 +
     13 +float smooth(float previous, float next, float amount) {
     14 +  return previous * amount + next * (1.0f - amount);
     15 +}
     16 +
     17 +float confidenceWeight(Confidence confidence) {
     18 +  switch (confidence) {
     19 +    case Confidence::High: return 1.0f;
     20 +    case Confidence::Moderate: return 0.68f;
     21 +    case Confidence::Low: return 0.38f;
     22 +  }
     23 +  return 0.38f;
     24 +}
     25 +
     26 +} // namespace
     27 +
     28 +void AnalysisEngine::prepare(double sampleRate) {
     29 +  sampleRate_ = sampleRate > 0.0 ? sampleRate : 44100.0;
     30 +  reset();
     31 +}
     32 +
     33 +void AnalysisEngine::reset() {
     34 +  live_ = {};
     35 +  smoothed_ = {};
     36 +}
     37 +
     38 +float AnalysisEngine::linearToDb(float value) {
     39 +  return 20.0f * std::log10(std::max(value, 0.0000316f));
     40 +}
     41 +
     42 +float AnalysisEngine::deviationOutsideCorridor(float value, float target, float tolerance, float criticalRange)
          {
     43 +  const auto miss = std::max(std::abs(value - target) - tolerance, 0.0f);
     44 +  const auto normalized = miss / std::max(criticalRange, 0.0001f);
     45 +  return clamp01(normalized * normalized * (3.0f - 2.0f * clamp01(normalized)));
     46 +}
     47 +
     48 +DomainAlignment AnalysisEngine::makeDomain(float error01, float primary, float secondary, std::string summary,
         float confidenceSeed) {
     49 +  DomainAlignment domain;
     50 +  domain.error01 = clamp01(error01);
     51 +  domain.alignment01 = 1.0f - domain.error01;
     52 +  domain.severity = severityForError(domain.error01);
     53 +  domain.confidence = confidenceForPersistence(confidenceSeed);
     54 +  domain.rawPrimaryMetric = primary;
     55 +  domain.rawSecondaryMetric = secondary;
     56 +  domain.summary = std::move(summary);
     57 +  return domain;
     58 +}
     59 +
     60 +void AnalysisEngine::pushAudioBlock(const juce::AudioBuffer<float>& buffer) {
     61 +  const auto channels = buffer.getNumChannels();
     62 +  const auto samples = buffer.getNumSamples();
     63 +  if (channels == 0 || samples == 0) return;
     64 +
     65 +  double sumSquares = 0.0;
     66 +  double peak = 0.0;
     67 +  double leftEnergy = 0.0;
     68 +  double rightEnergy = 0.0;
     69 +  double midEnergy = 0.0;
     70 +  double sideEnergy = 0.0;
     71 +  double corrNum = 0.0;
     72 +  double transient = 0.0;
     73 +  double lowMotion = 0.0;
     74 +  double highMotion = 0.0;
     75 +  float prevMono = 0.0f;
     76 +
     77 +  const auto* left = buffer.getReadPointer(0);
     78 +  const auto* right = channels > 1 ? buffer.getReadPointer(1) : left;
     79 +
     80 +  for (int i = 0; i < samples; ++i) {
     81 +    const auto l = left[i];
     82 +    const auto r = right[i];
     83 +    const auto mono = 0.5f * (l + r);
     84 +    const auto side = 0.5f * (l - r);
     85 +    sumSquares += 0.5 * (static_cast<double>(l) * l + static_cast<double>(r) * r);
     86 +    leftEnergy += static_cast<double>(l) * l;
     87 +    rightEnergy += static_cast<double>(r) * r;
     88 +    midEnergy += static_cast<double>(mono) * mono;
     89 +    sideEnergy += static_cast<double>(side) * side;
     90 +    corrNum += static_cast<double>(l) * r;
     91 +    peak = std::max({peak, std::abs(static_cast<double>(l)), std::abs(static_cast<double>(r))});
     92 +    transient += std::abs(mono - prevMono);
     93 +    prevMono = mono;
     94 +
     95 +    if (i > 0) {
     96 +      const auto slow = 0.985f * prevMono + 0.015f * mono;
     97 +      lowMotion += std::abs(slow);
     98 +      highMotion += std::abs(mono - slow);
     99 +    }
    100 +  }
    101 +
    102 +  const auto sampleCount = std::max(samples, 1);
    103 +  const auto rms = safeSqrt(static_cast<float>(sumSquares / sampleCount));
    104 +  const auto leftRms = safeSqrt(static_cast<float>(leftEnergy / sampleCount));
    105 +  const auto rightRms = safeSqrt(static_cast<float>(rightEnergy / sampleCount));
    106 +  const auto denom = std::max(leftRms * rightRms * sampleCount, 0.000001f);
    107 +  const auto correlation = std::clamp(static_cast<float>(corrNum) / denom, -1.0f, 1.0f);
    108 +  const auto width = clamp01(safeSqrt(static_cast<float>(sideEnergy / std::max(midEnergy + sideEnergy, 0.000001
         ))));
    109 +  const auto crest = linearToDb(static_cast<float>(peak)) - linearToDb(rms);
    110 +  const auto tilt = clamp01(static_cast<float>(highMotion / std::max(lowMotion + highMotion, 0.000001)));
    111 +
    112 +  live_.rmsDb = linearToDb(rms);
    113 +  live_.peakDb = linearToDb(static_cast<float>(peak));
    114 +  live_.crestDb = std::clamp(crest, 0.0f, 24.0f);
    115 +  live_.stereoWidth = width;
    116 +  live_.correlation = correlation;
    117 +  live_.spectralTilt = tilt;
    118 +  live_.transientDensity = clamp01(static_cast<float>(transient / sampleCount) * 9.0f);
    119 +  live_.signal01 = clamp01((live_.rmsDb + 60.0f) / 48.0f);
    120 +
    121 +  const auto amount = live_.signal01 > 0.02f ? smoothing_ : 0.98f;
    122 +  smoothed_.rmsDb = smooth(smoothed_.rmsDb, live_.rmsDb, amount);
    123 +  smoothed_.peakDb = smooth(smoothed_.peakDb, live_.peakDb, amount);
    124 +  smoothed_.crestDb = smooth(smoothed_.crestDb, live_.crestDb, amount);
    125 +  smoothed_.stereoWidth = smooth(smoothed_.stereoWidth, live_.stereoWidth, amount);
    126 +  smoothed_.correlation = smooth(smoothed_.correlation, live_.correlation, amount);
    127 +  smoothed_.spectralTilt = smooth(smoothed_.spectralTilt, live_.spectralTilt, amount);
    128 +  smoothed_.transientDensity = smooth(smoothed_.transientDensity, live_.transientDensity, amount);
    129 +  smoothed_.signal01 = smooth(smoothed_.signal01, live_.signal01, amount);
    130 +}
    131 +
    132 +HaloState AnalysisEngine::snapshot() const {
    133 +  return buildHaloState();
    134 +}
    135 +
    136 +HaloState AnalysisEngine::buildHaloState() const {
    137 +  HaloState state;
    138 +  const auto confidence = clamp01(smoothed_.signal01 * 1.35f);
    139 +
    140 +  const auto toneTiltError = deviationOutsideCorridor(smoothed_.spectralTilt, 0.48f, 0.16f, 0.36f);
    141 +  const auto loudnessError = 0.55f * deviationOutsideCorridor(smoothed_.rmsDb, -16.0f, 5.0f, 18.0f)
    142 +                           + 0.45f * deviationOutsideCorridor(smoothed_.peakDb, -1.0f, 1.5f, 10.0f);
    143 +  const auto dynamicsError = 0.58f * deviationOutsideCorridor(smoothed_.crestDb, 10.0f, 4.0f, 12.0f)
    144 +                           + 0.42f * deviationOutsideCorridor(smoothed_.transientDensity, 0.42f, 0.25f, 0.65f);
    145 +  const auto stereoWidthError = deviationOutsideCorridor(smoothed_.stereoWidth, 0.52f, 0.24f, 0.5f);
    146 +  const auto phaseError = smoothed_.correlation < 0.0f ? clamp01(-smoothed_.correlation) : 0.0f;
    147 +  const auto stereoError = 0.72f * stereoWidthError + 0.28f * phaseError;
    148 +
    149 +  state.tone = makeDomain(toneTiltError, smoothed_.spectralTilt, smoothed_.rmsDb, "Spectral shape compared agai
         nst a balanced production corridor.", confidence);
    150 +  state.stereo = makeDomain(stereoError, smoothed_.stereoWidth, smoothed_.correlation, "Width and mono safety a
         bove the protected low end.", confidence);
    151 +  state.loudness = makeDomain(loudnessError, smoothed_.rmsDb, smoothed_.peakDb, "Working loudness and headroom
         relative to a mix-stage target.", confidence);
    152 +  state.dynamics = makeDomain(dynamicsError, smoothed_.crestDb, smoothed_.transientDensity, "Crest, transient m
         otion, and controlled punch.", confidence);
    153 +
    154 +  const auto totalError = 0.35f * state.tone.error01 + 0.25f * state.stereo.error01
    155 +                        + 0.20f * state.loudness.error01 + 0.20f * state.dynamics.error01;
    156 +  state.totalAlignment01 = 1.0f - clamp01(totalError);
    157 +
    158 +  auto addFix = [&](Domain domain, const char* title, const char* cause, const char* nextStep, const DomainAlig
         nment& alignment) {
    159 +    FixItem item;
    160 +    item.title = title;
    161 +    item.cause = cause;
    162 +    item.nextStep = nextStep;
    163 +    item.severity = alignment.severity;
    164 +    item.confidence = alignment.confidence;
    165 +    item.impactDomain = domain;
    166 +    item.priority = alignment.error01 * confidenceWeight(alignment.confidence);
    167 +    state.rankedFixes.push_back(std::move(item));
    168 +  };
    169 +
    170 +  if (state.stereo.error01 > 0.18f) {
    171 +    if (smoothed_.correlation < -0.05f) {
    172 +      addFix(Domain::Stereo, "Phase Risk", "Side energy is fighting mono collapse.", "Control widened layers an
         d check the chorus in mono.", state.stereo);
    173 +    } else {
    174 +      addFix(Domain::Stereo, "Stereo Image Needs Shape", "Width is outside the reference corridor.", "Widen onl
         y upper detail or narrow unstable side content.", state.stereo);
    175 +    }
    176 +  }
    177 +  if (state.tone.error01 > 0.18f) {
    178 +    addFix(Domain::Tone, "Tone Balance Drift", "The spectral shape is leaning away from the target corridor.",
         "Trim the dominant buildup before adding more top or sub.", state.tone);
    179 +  }
    180 +  if (state.loudness.error01 > 0.18f) {
    181 +    addFix(Domain::Loudness, "Headroom Relationship Off", "Level and peak behavior are not sitting in the mix-s
         tage pocket.", "Set the mix bus for cleaner headroom before final limiting.", state.loudness);
    182 +  }
    183 +  if (state.dynamics.error01 > 0.18f) {
    184 +    addFix(Domain::Dynamics, "Punch Needs Rebalancing", "Crest and transient motion are outside the controlled
         range.", "Ease compression or restore attack on the sources carrying movement.", state.dynamics);
    185 +  }
    186 +
    187 +  std::sort(state.rankedFixes.begin(), state.rankedFixes.end(), [](const auto& a, const auto& b) {
    188 +    return a.priority > b.priority;
    189 +  });
    190 +
    191 +  if (smoothed_.signal01 < 0.02f) {
    192 +    state.primaryTitle = "Waiting For Signal";
    193 +    state.primaryCause = "Route audio through Aifred to start the Halo read.";
    194 +    state.primarySeverity = Severity::Minor;
    195 +    state.primaryConfidence = Confidence::Low;
    196 +    state.rankedFixes.clear();
    197 +    return state;
    198 +  }
    199 +
    200 +  if (state.totalAlignment01 >= 0.82f) {
    201 +    state.primaryTitle = "Close To Reference";
    202 +    state.primaryCause = "Tone, stereo, loudness, and dynamics are staying inside the working corridor.";
    203 +    state.primarySeverity = Severity::Minor;
    204 +    state.primaryConfidence = Confidence::High;
    205 +    return state;
    206 +  }
    207 +
    208 +  if (!state.rankedFixes.empty()) {
    209 +    const auto& top = state.rankedFixes.front();
    210 +    state.primaryTitle = top.title;
    211 +    state.primaryCause = top.cause;
    212 +    state.primarySeverity = top.severity;
    213 +    state.primaryConfidence = top.confidence;
    214 +  }
    215 +
    216 +  return state;
    217 +}
    218 +
    219 +} // namespace aifred

    113 +void AifredAudioProcessorEditor::drawHalo(juce::Graphics& g, juce::Rectangle<int> bounds, const HaloState& stat
         e) {
    114 +  drawPanel(g, bounds.toFloat(), 8.0f);
    115 +  auto haloBounds = bounds.reduced(28);
    116 +  const auto size = std::min(haloBounds.getWidth(), haloBounds.getHeight());
    117 +  auto square = juce::Rectangle<int>(0, 0, size, size).withCentre(haloBounds.getCentre());
    118 +  auto area = square.toFloat().reduced(24.0f);
    119 +  auto centre = area.getCentre();
    120 +  auto radius = std::min(area.getWidth(), area.getHeight()) * 0.47f;
    121 +
    122 +  g.setColour(Colours::cyan.withAlpha(0.08f));
    123 +  g.fillEllipse(centre.x - radius, centre.y - radius, radius * 2.0f, radius * 2.0f);
    124 +
    125 +  const std::array<const DomainAlignment*, 4> domains = {&state.tone, &state.stereo, &state.loudness, &state.dy
         namics};
    126 +  const std::array<float, 4> starts = {-155.0f, -62.0f, 31.0f, 124.0f};
    127 +  for (int i = 0; i < 4; ++i) {
    128 +    auto alignment = domains[static_cast<size_t>(i)]->alignment01;
    129 +    auto colour = colourForAlignment(alignment);
    130 +    auto arcRadius = radius - static_cast<float>(i % 2) * 13.0f;
    131 +    juce::Path bg;
    132 +    bg.addCentredArc(centre.x, centre.y, arcRadius, arcRadius, 0.0f,
    133 +                     juce::degreesToRadians(starts[static_cast<size_t>(i)]),
    134 +                     juce::degreesToRadians(starts[static_cast<size_t>(i)] + 72.0f), true);
    135 +    g.setColour(Colours::line.withAlpha(0.45f));
    136 +    g.strokePath(bg, juce::PathStrokeType(8.0f));
    137 +
    138 +    juce::Path arc;
    139 +    arc.addCentredArc(centre.x, centre.y, arcRadius, arcRadius, 0.0f,
    140 +                      juce::degreesToRadians(starts[static_cast<size_t>(i)]),
    141 +                      juce::degreesToRadians(starts[static_cast<size_t>(i)] + 72.0f * alignment), true);
    142 +    g.setColour(colour.withAlpha(0.92f));
    143 +    g.strokePath(arc, juce::PathStrokeType(8.0f, juce::PathStrokeType::curved, juce::PathStrokeType::rounded));
    144 +  }
    145 +
    146 +  auto card = juce::Rectangle<float>(centre.x - 190.0f, centre.y - 78.0f, 380.0f, 156.0f);
    147 +  drawPanel(g, card, 8.0f);
    148 +  g.setFont(juce::FontOptions(18.0f, juce::Font::bold));
    149 +  g.setColour(Colours::ink);
    150 +  g.drawText(state.primaryTitle, card.removeFromTop(38.0f), juce::Justification::centred);
    151 +  g.setFont(juce::FontOptions(43.0f, juce::Font::bold));
    152 +  g.setColour(colourForAlignment(state.totalAlignment01));
    153 +  g.drawText(pct(state.totalAlignment01), card.removeFromTop(58.0f), juce::Justification::centred);
    154 +  g.setFont(juce::FontOptions(13.0f));
    155 +  g.setColour(Colours::muted);
    156 +  g.drawFittedText(juce::String(state.primaryCause), card.toNearestInt().reduced(18, 0), juce::Justification::c
         entred, 2);
    157 +
    158 +  g.setFont(juce::FontOptions(13.0f, juce::Font::bold));
    159 +  g.setColour(Colours::muted);
    160 +  g.drawText("Alignment Score + domain rings + ranked cause-based fixes", bounds.removeFromBottom(28), juce::Ju
         stification::centred);
    161 +}

    215 +void AifredAudioProcessorEditor::drawMiniGraph(juce::Graphics& g, juce::Rectangle<int> bounds, const HaloState&
          state) {
    216 +  drawPanel(g, bounds.toFloat(), 8.0f);
    217 +  auto inner = bounds.reduced(16);
    218 +  g.setFont(juce::FontOptions(17.0f, juce::Font::bold));
    219 +  g.setColour(Colours::ink);
    220 +  g.drawText("MIX SIGNATURE", inner.removeFromTop(30), juce::Justification::centredLeft);
    221 +  auto graph = inner.reduced(4, 10).toFloat();
    222 +  g.setColour(Colours::line.withAlpha(0.6f));
    223 +  g.drawRoundedRectangle(graph, 8.0f, 1.0f);
    224 +  auto centre = graph.getCentre();
    225 +  const std::array<float, 4> values = {state.tone.alignment01, state.stereo.alignment01, state.loudness.alignme
         nt01, state.dynamics.alignment01};
    226 +  juce::Path path;
    227 +  for (int i = 0; i < 4; ++i) {
    228 +    const auto angle = juce::MathConstants<float>::twoPi * static_cast<float>(i) / 4.0f - juce::MathConstants<f
         loat>::halfPi;
    229 +    const auto radius = std::min(graph.getWidth(), graph.getHeight()) * 0.42f * values[static_cast<size_t>(i)];
    230 +    const auto point = juce::Point<float>(centre.x + std::cos(angle) * radius, centre.y + std::sin(angle) * rad
         ius);
    231 +    if (i == 0) path.startNewSubPath(point); else path.lineTo(point);
    232 +  }
    233 +  path.closeSubPath();
    234 +  g.setColour(Colours::cyan.withAlpha(0.18f));
    235 +  g.fillPath(path);
    236 +  g.setColour(Colours::cyan.withAlpha(0.92f));
    237 +  g.strokePath(path, juce::PathStrokeType(2.0f));
    238 +}

     7 +float clamp01(float value) {
     8 +  return std::clamp(value, 0.0f, 1.0f);
     9 +}
    10 +
    11 +Severity severityForError(float error01) {
    12 +  const auto error = clamp01(error01);
    13 +  if (error >= 0.65f) return Severity::Critical;
    14 +  if (error >= 0.40f) return Severity::High;
    15 +  if (error >= 0.20f) return Severity::Moderate;
    16 +  return Severity::Minor;
    17 +}
    18 +
    19 +Confidence confidenceForPersistence(float persistence01) {
    20 +  const auto persistence = clamp01(persistence01);
    21 +  if (persistence >= 0.72f) return Confidence::High;
    22 +  if (persistence >= 0.42f) return Confidence::Moderate;
    23 +  return Confidence::Low;
    24 +}
    25 +
    26 +const char* domainName(Domain domain) {
    27 +  switch (domain) {
    28 +    case Domain::Tone: return "Tone";
    29 +    case Domain::Stereo: return "Stereo";
    30 +    case Domain::Loudness: return "Loudness";
    31 +    case Domain::Dynamics: return "Dynamics";
    32 +  }
    33 +  return "Domain";
    34 +}
    35 +
    36 +const char* severityName(Severity severity) {
    37 +  switch (severity) {
    38 +    case Severity::Minor: return "Minor";
    39 +    case Severity::Moderate: return "Moderate";
    40 +    case Severity::High: return "High";
    41 +    case Severity::Critical: return "Critical";
    42 +  }
    43 +  return "Minor";
    44 +}
    45 +
    46 +const char* confidenceName(Confidence confidence) {
    47 +  switch (confidence) {
    48 +    case Confidence::Low: return "Low";
    49 +    case Confidence::Moderate: return "Moderate";
    50 +    case Confidence::High: return "High";
    51 +  }
    52 +  return "Low";

  └ plugin-aifred\Source\AnalysisEngine.cpp (+203 -0)
      1 +#include "AnalysisEngine.h"
      2 +
      3 +#include <algorithm>
      4 +#include <cmath>
      5 +
      6 +namespace aifred {
      7 +namespace {
      8 +
      9 +float safeSqrt(float value) {
     10 +  return std::sqrt(std::max(value, 0.0f));
     11 +}
     12 +
     13 +float smooth(float previous, float next, float amount) {
     14 +  return previous * amount + next * (1.0f - amount);
     15 +}
     16 +
     17 +float confidenceWeight(Confidence confidence) {
     18 +  switch (confidence) {
     19 +    case Confidence::High: return 1.0f;
     20 +    case Confidence::Moderate: return 0.68f;
     21 +    case Confidence::Low: return 0.38f;
     22 +  }
     23 +  return 0.38f;
     24 +}
     25 +
     26 +} // namespace
     27 +
     28 +void AnalysisEngine::prepare(double sampleRate) {
     29 +  sampleRate_ = sampleRate > 0.0 ? sampleRate : 44100.0;
     30 +  reset();
     31 +}
     32 +
     33 +void AnalysisEngine::reset() {
     34 +  live_ = {};
     35 +  smoothed_ = {};
     36 +}
     37 +
     38 +float AnalysisEngine::linearToDb(float value) {
     39 +  return 20.0f * std::log10(std::max(value, 0.0000316f));
     40 +}
     41 +
     42 +float AnalysisEngine::deviationOutsideCorridor(float value, float target, float tolerance, float criticalRange)
          {
     43 +  const auto miss = std::max(std::abs(value - target) - tolerance, 0.0f);
     44 +  const auto normalized = miss / std::max(criticalRange, 0.0001f);
     45 +  return clamp01(normalized * normalized * (3.0f - 2.0f * clamp01(normalized)));
     46 +}
     47 +
     48 +DomainAlignment AnalysisEngine::makeDomain(float error01, float primary, float secondary, std::string summary,
         float confidenceSeed) {
     49 +  DomainAlignment domain;
     50 +  domain.error01 = clamp01(error01);
     51 +  domain.alignment01 = 1.0f - domain.error01;
     52 +  domain.severity = severityForError(domain.error01);
     53 +  domain.confidence = confidenceForPersistence(confidenceSeed);
     54 +  domain.rawPrimaryMetric = primary;
     55 +  domain.rawSecondaryMetric = secondary;
     56 +  domain.summary = std::move(summary);
     57 +  return domain;
     58 +}
     59 +
     60 +void AnalysisEngine::pushAudioBlock(const juce::AudioBuffer<float>& buffer) {
     61 +  const auto channels = buffer.getNumChannels();
     62 +  const auto samples = buffer.getNumSamples();
     63 +  if (channels == 0 || samples == 0) return;
     64 +
     65 +  double sumSquares = 0.0;
     66 +  double peak = 0.0;
     67 +  double leftEnergy = 0.0;
     68 +  double rightEnergy = 0.0;
     69 +  double midEnergy = 0.0;
     70 +  double sideEnergy = 0.0;
     71 +  double corrNum = 0.0;
     72 +  double transient = 0.0;
     73 +  double lowMotion = 0.0;
     74 +  double highMotion = 0.0;
     75 +  float prevMono = 0.0f;
     76 +
     77 +  const auto* left = buffer.getReadPointer(0);
     78 +  const auto* right = channels > 1 ? buffer.getReadPointer(1) : left;
     79 +
     80 +  for (int i = 0; i < samples; ++i) {
     81 +    const auto l = left[i];
     82 +    const auto r = right[i];
     83 +    const auto mono = 0.5f * (l + r);
     84 +    const auto side = 0.5f * (l - r);
     85 +    sumSquares += 0.5 * (static_cast<double>(l) * l + static_cast<double>(r) * r);
     86 +    leftEnergy += static_cast<double>(l) * l;
     87 +    rightEnergy += static_cast<double>(r) * r;
     88 +    midEnergy += static_cast<double>(mono) * mono;
     89 +    sideEnergy += static_cast<double>(side) * side;
     90 +    corrNum += static_cast<double>(l) * r;
     91 +    peak = std::max({peak, std::abs(static_cast<double>(l)), std::abs(static_cast<double>(r))});
     92 +    transient += std::abs(mono - prevMono);
     93 +    prevMono = mono;
     94 +
     95 +    const auto slow = 0.985f * prevMono + 0.015f * mono;
     96 +    lowMotion += std::abs(slow);
     97 +    highMotion += std::abs(mono - slow);
     98 +  }
     99 +
    100 +  const auto sampleCount = std::max(samples, 1);
    101 +  const auto rms = safeSqrt(static_cast<float>(sumSquares / sampleCount));
    102 +  const auto leftRms = safeSqrt(static_cast<float>(leftEnergy / sampleCount));
    103 +  const auto rightRms = safeSqrt(static_cast<float>(rightEnergy / sampleCount));
    104 +  const auto denom = std::max(leftRms * rightRms * static_cast<float>(sampleCount), 0.000001f);
    105 +  const auto correlation = std::clamp(static_cast<float>(corrNum) / denom, -1.0f, 1.0f);
    106 +  const auto width = clamp01(safeSqrt(static_cast<float>(sideEnergy / std::max(midEnergy + sideEnergy, 0.000001
         ))));
    107 +  const auto crest = linearToDb(static_cast<float>(peak)) - linearToDb(rms);
    108 +  const auto tilt = clamp01(static_cast<float>(highMotion / std::max(lowMotion + highMotion, 0.000001)));
    109 +
    110 +  live_.rmsDb = linearToDb(rms);
    111 +  live_.peakDb = linearToDb(static_cast<float>(peak));
    112 +  live_.crestDb = std::clamp(crest, 0.0f, 24.0f);
    113 +  live_.stereoWidth = width;
    114 +  live_.correlation = correlation;
    115 +  live_.spectralTilt = tilt;
    116 +  live_.transientDensity = clamp01(static_cast<float>(transient / sampleCount) * 9.0f);
    117 +  live_.signal01 = clamp01((live_.rmsDb + 60.0f) / 48.0f);
    118 +
    119 +  const auto amount = live_.signal01 > 0.02f ? smoothing_ : 0.98f;
    120 +  smoothed_.rmsDb = smooth(smoothed_.rmsDb, live_.rmsDb, amount);
    121 +  smoothed_.peakDb = smooth(smoothed_.peakDb, live_.peakDb, amount);
    122 +  smoothed_.crestDb = smooth(smoothed_.crestDb, live_.crestDb, amount);
    123 +  smoothed_.stereoWidth = smooth(smoothed_.stereoWidth, live_.stereoWidth, amount);
    124 +  smoothed_.correlation = smooth(smoothed_.correlation, live_.correlation, amount);
    125 +  smoothed_.spectralTilt = smooth(smoothed_.spectralTilt, live_.spectralTilt, amount);
    126 +  smoothed_.transientDensity = smooth(smoothed_.transientDensity, live_.transientDensity, amount);
    127 +  smoothed_.signal01 = smooth(smoothed_.signal01, live_.signal01, amount);
    128 +}
    129 +
    130 +HaloState AnalysisEngine::snapshot() const {
    131 +  return buildHaloState();
    132 +}
    133 +
    134 +HaloState AnalysisEngine::buildHaloState() const {
    135 +  HaloState state;
    136 +  const auto confidence = clamp01(smoothed_.signal01 * 1.35f);
    137 +
    138 +  const auto toneError = deviationOutsideCorridor(smoothed_.spectralTilt, 0.48f, 0.16f, 0.36f);
    139 +  const auto loudnessError = 0.55f * deviationOutsideCorridor(smoothed_.rmsDb, -16.0f, 5.0f, 18.0f)
    140 +                           + 0.45f * deviationOutsideCorridor(smoothed_.peakDb, -1.0f, 1.5f, 10.0f);
    141 +  const auto dynamicsError = 0.58f * deviationOutsideCorridor(smoothed_.crestDb, 10.0f, 4.0f, 12.0f)
    142 +                           + 0.42f * deviationOutsideCorridor(smoothed_.transientDensity, 0.42f, 0.25f, 0.65f);
    143 +  const auto stereoWidthError = deviationOutsideCorridor(smoothed_.stereoWidth, 0.52f, 0.24f, 0.5f);
    144 +  const auto phaseError = smoothed_.correlation < 0.0f ? clamp01(-smoothed_.correlation) : 0.0f;
    145 +  const auto stereoError = 0.72f * stereoWidthError + 0.28f * phaseError;
    146 +
    147 +  state.tone = makeDomain(toneError, smoothed_.spectralTilt, smoothed_.rmsDb, "Spectral shape against a balance
         d production corridor.", confidence);
    148 +  state.stereo = makeDomain(stereoError, smoothed_.stereoWidth, smoothed_.correlation, "Width and mono safety a
         bove the protected low end.", confidence);
    149 +  state.loudness = makeDomain(loudnessError, smoothed_.rmsDb, smoothed_.peakDb, "Working loudness and headroom
         relative to a mix-stage target.", confidence);
    150 +  state.dynamics = makeDomain(dynamicsError, smoothed_.crestDb, smoothed_.transientDensity, "Crest, transient m
         otion, and controlled punch.", confidence);
    151 +
    152 +  const auto totalError = 0.35f * state.tone.error01 + 0.25f * state.stereo.error01
    153 +                        + 0.20f * state.loudness.error01 + 0.20f * state.dynamics.error01;
    154 +  state.totalAlignment01 = 1.0f - clamp01(totalError);
    155 +
    156 +  auto addFix = [&](Domain domain, const char* title, const char* cause, const char* nextStep, const DomainAlig
         nment& alignment) {
    157 +    FixItem item;
    158 +    item.title = title;
    159 +    item.cause = cause;
    160 +    item.nextStep = nextStep;
    161 +    item.severity = alignment.severity;
    162 +    item.confidence = alignment.confidence;
    163 +    item.impactDomain = domain;
    164 +    item.priority = alignment.error01 * confidenceWeight(alignment.confidence);
    165 +    state.rankedFixes.push_back(std::move(item));
    166 +  };
    167 +
    168 +  if (state.stereo.error01 > 0.18f) addFix(Domain::Stereo, "Stereo Image Needs Shape", "Width and mono safety a
         re outside the reference corridor.", "Widen upper detail or narrow unstable side content.", state.stereo);
    169 +  if (state.tone.error01 > 0.18f) addFix(Domain::Tone, "Tone Balance Drift", "The spectral shape is leaning awa
         y from the target corridor.", "Trim the dominant buildup before adding more top or sub.", state.tone);
    170 +  if (state.loudness.error01 > 0.18f) addFix(Domain::Loudness, "Headroom Relationship Off", "Level and peak beh
         avior are not sitting in the mix-stage pocket.", "Set the mix bus for cleaner headroom before final limiting.",
          state.loudness);
    171 +  if (state.dynamics.error01 > 0.18f) addFix(Domain::Dynamics, "Punch Needs Rebalancing", "Crest and transient
         motion are outside the controlled range.", "Ease compression or restore attack on the sources carrying movement
         .", state.dynamics);
    172 +
    173 +  std::sort(state.rankedFixes.begin(), state.rankedFixes.end(), [](const auto& a, const auto& b) {
    174 +    return a.priority > b.priority;
    175 +  });
    176 +
    177 +  if (smoothed_.signal01 < 0.02f) {
    178 +    state.primaryTitle = "Waiting For Signal";
    179 +    state.primaryCause = "Route audio through Aifred to start the Halo read.";
    180 +    state.rankedFixes.clear();
    181 +    return state;
    182 +  }
    183 +
    184 +  if (state.totalAlignment01 >= 0.82f) {
    185 +    state.primaryTitle = "Close To Reference";
    186 +    state.primaryCause = "Tone, stereo, loudness, and dynamics are staying inside the working corridor.";
    187 +    state.primarySeverity = Severity::Minor;
    188 +    state.primaryConfidence = Confidence::High;
    189 +    return state;
    190 +  }
    191 +
    192 +  if (!state.rankedFixes.empty()) {
    193 +    const auto& top = state.rankedFixes.front();
    194 +    state.primaryTitle = top.title;
    195 +    state.primaryCause = top.cause;
    196 +    state.primarySeverity = top.severity;
    197 +    state.primaryConfidence = top.confidence;
    198 +  }
    199 +
    200 +  return state;
    201 +}
    202 +
    203 +} // namespace aifred

    115 +void AifredAudioProcessorEditor::drawHalo(juce::Graphics& g, juce::Rectangle<int> bounds, const HaloState& stat
         e) {
    116 +  drawPanel(g, bounds.toFloat(), 8.0f);
    117 +  auto haloBounds = bounds.reduced(28);
    118 +  const auto size = std::min(haloBounds.getWidth(), haloBounds.getHeight());
    119 +  auto square = juce::Rectangle<int>(0, 0, size, size).withCentre(haloBounds.getCentre());
    120 +  auto area = square.toFloat().reduced(24.0f);
    121 +  auto centre = area.getCentre();
    122 +  auto radius = std::min(area.getWidth(), area.getHeight()) * 0.47f;
    123 +
    124 +  g.setColour(Colours::cyan.withAlpha(0.08f));
    125 +  g.fillEllipse(centre.x - radius, centre.y - radius, radius * 2.0f, radius * 2.0f);
    126 +
    127 +  const std::array<const DomainAlignment*, 4> domains = {&state.tone, &state.stereo, &state.loudness, &state.dy
         namics};
    128 +  const std::array<float, 4> starts = {-155.0f, -62.0f, 31.0f, 124.0f};
    129 +  for (int i = 0; i < 4; ++i) {
    130 +    auto alignment = domains[static_cast<size_t>(i)]->alignment01;
    131 +    auto colour = colourForAlignment(alignment);
    132 +    auto arcRadius = radius - static_cast<float>(i % 2) * 13.0f;
    133 +    juce::Path bg;
    134 +    bg.addCentredArc(centre.x, centre.y, arcRadius, arcRadius, 0.0f,
    135 +                     juce::degreesToRadians(starts[static_cast<size_t>(i)]),
    136 +                     juce::degreesToRadians(starts[static_cast<size_t>(i)] + 72.0f), true);
    137 +    g.setColour(Colours::line.withAlpha(0.45f));
    138 +    g.strokePath(bg, juce::PathStrokeType(8.0f));
    139 +
    140 +    juce::Path arc;
    141 +    arc.addCentredArc(centre.x, centre.y, arcRadius, arcRadius, 0.0f,
    142 +                      juce::degreesToRadians(starts[static_cast<size_t>(i)]),
    143 +                      juce::degreesToRadians(starts[static_cast<size_t>(i)] + 72.0f * alignment), true);
    144 +    g.setColour(colour.withAlpha(0.92f));
    145 +    g.strokePath(arc, juce::PathStrokeType(8.0f, juce::PathStrokeType::curved, juce::PathStrokeType::rounded));
    146 +  }
    147 +
    148 +  auto card = juce::Rectangle<float>(centre.x - 190.0f, centre.y - 78.0f, 380.0f, 156.0f);
    149 +  drawPanel(g, card, 8.0f);
    150 +  g.setFont(juce::FontOptions(18.0f, juce::Font::bold));
    151 +  g.setColour(Colours::ink);
    152 +  g.drawText(state.primaryTitle, card.removeFromTop(38.0f), juce::Justification::centred);
    153 +  g.setFont(juce::FontOptions(43.0f, juce::Font::bold));
    154 +  g.setColour(colourForAlignment(state.totalAlignment01));
    155 +  g.drawText(pct(state.totalAlignment01), card.removeFromTop(58.0f), juce::Justification::centred);
    156 +  g.setFont(juce::FontOptions(13.0f));
    157 +  g.setColour(Colours::muted);
    158 +  g.drawFittedText(juce::String(state.primaryCause), card.toNearestInt().reduced(18, 0), juce::Justification::c
         entred, 2);
    159 +
    160 +  g.setFont(juce::FontOptions(13.0f, juce::Font::bold));
    161 +  g.setColour(Colours::muted);
    162 +  g.drawText("Alignment Score + domain rings + ranked cause-based fixes", bounds.removeFromBottom(28), juce::Ju
         stification::centred);
    163 +}

         e, const DomainAlignment& alignment) {

    184 +void AifredAudioProcessorEditor::drawFixList(juce::Graphics& g, juce::Rectangle<int> bounds, const HaloState& s
         tate) {

    217 +void AifredAudioProcessorEditor::drawMixSignature(juce::Graphics& g, juce::Rectangle<int> bounds, const HaloSta
         te& state) {
    218 +  drawPanel(g, bounds.toFloat(), 8.0f);
    219 +  auto inner = bounds.reduced(16);
    220 +  g.setFont(juce::FontOptions(17.0f, juce::Font::bold));
    221 +  g.setColour(Colours::ink);
    222 +  g.drawText("MIX SIGNATURE", inner.removeFromTop(30), juce::Justification::centredLeft);
    223 +  auto graph = inner.reduced(4, 10).toFloat();
    224 +  g.setColour(Colours::line.withAlpha(0.6f));
    225 +  g.drawRoundedRectangle(graph, 8.0f, 1.0f);
    226 +  auto centre = graph.getCentre();
    227 +  const std::array<float, 4> values = {state.tone.alignment01, state.stereo.alignment01, state.loudness.alignme
         nt01, state.dynamics.alignment01};
    228 +  juce::Path path;
    229 +  for (int i = 0; i < 4; ++i) {
    230 +    const auto angle = juce::MathConstants<float>::twoPi * static_cast<float>(i) / 4.0f - juce::MathConstants<f
         loat>::halfPi;
    231 +    const auto radius = std::min(graph.getWidth(), graph.getHeight()) * 0.42f * values[static_cast<size_t>(i)];
    232 +    const auto point = juce::Point<float>(centre.x + std::cos(angle) * radius, centre.y + std::sin(angle) * rad
         ius);
    233 +    if (i == 0) path.startNewSubPath(point); else path.lineTo(point);
    234 +  }
    235 +  path.closeSubPath();
    236 +  g.setColour(Colours::cyan.withAlpha(0.18f));
    237 +  g.fillPath(path);
    238 +  g.setColour(Colours::cyan.withAlpha(0.92f));
    239 +  g.strokePath(path, juce::PathStrokeType(2.0f));
    240 +}
    241 +
    242 +} // namespace aifred

     50 +async function getJson(path, fallback) {
     51 +  try {
     52 +    const response = await fetch(apiUrl(path), { cache: "no-store" });
     53 +    const payload = await response.json();
     54 +    if (response.ok) return payload;

     77 +    || "Aifred received the request, but the model returned no text.";

    105 +async function handleChat(request, env) {

    116 +  } catch (error) {
    117 +    return json({ ok: false, error: error.message || "chat provider failed" }, { status: 503 });
    118 +  }

     2 +
     3 +AIFRED is a fresh Windows-first VST3 and website build for North3rnLight3r. The plugin source in this repo is ne

        age, and asset choices.
     4 +
     5 +## Layout
     6 +
     7 +- `plugin-aifred/` contains the AIFRED VST3 source and mascot asset.
     8 +- `website/` contains the storefront, beat catalog assets, and Cloudflare Pages Functions.
     9 +- `android_admin/` contains the renamed AIFRED admin app configuration surface.
    10 +- `.github/workflows/build.yml` builds Windows, macOS, Ubuntu, and Arch Linux targets.
    11 +
    12 +## Windows VST3 Build
    13 +
    14 +Install Visual Studio with the Desktop development with C++ workload, CMake, Git, and Ninja. From a Visual Studi
        o developer shell:
    15 +
    16 +```powershell
    17 +cmake -S . -B build/aifred -G Ninja -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release
    18 +cmake --build build/aifred --parallel
    19 +./tools/package-aifred.ps1 -BuildRoot build/aifred -Platform windows
    20 +```
    21 +
    22 +The package script writes `dist/AIFRED-VST3-windows.zip`. Copy `Aifred.vst3` from that package to the Windows VS
        T3 folder and rescan in FL Studio.
    23 +
    24 +## Website Backend
    25 +
    26 +Cloudflare Pages should use `website/` as the project root. Secrets stay in Cloudflare environment variables:
    27 +
    28 +- `AIFRED_CHAT_PROVIDER`: `openai` or `ollama`
    29 +- `OPENAI_API_KEY`
    30 +- `OPENAI_MODEL`

    32 +- `OLLAMA_MODEL`
    33 +- `AIFRED_CONTACT_EMAIL`
    34 +
    35 +Catalog metadata is read from `website/assets/data/beat_catalog.json`, and beat files are served from `website/a
        ssets/audio/catalog/`.

     24 +function sendJson(response, status, body) {
     25 +  response.writeHead(status, {
     26 +    "content-type": "application/json; charset=utf-8",
     27 +    "cache-control": "no-store"
     28 +  });
     29 +  response.end(JSON.stringify(body));
     30 +}
     31 +
     32 +async function readRequestJson(request) {
     33 +  const chunks = [];
     34 +  for await (const chunk of request) chunks.push(chunk);
     35 +  const raw = Buffer.concat(chunks).toString("utf8");
     36 +  if (!raw.trim()) return {};
     37 +  return JSON.parse(raw);
     38 +}
     39 +
     40 +async function routeApi(request, response, url) {
     41 +  if (url.pathname === "/api/v1/health") {
     42 +    return sendJson(response, 200, { ok: true, service: "AIFRED local website backend" });
     43 +  }
     44 +
     45 +  if (url.pathname === "/api/v1/catalog/list") {
     46 +    const raw = await readFile(path.join(siteRoot, "assets", "data", "beat_catalog.json"), "utf8");
     47 +    return sendJson(response, 200, { ok: true, tracks: JSON.parse(raw) });
     48 +  }
     49 +
     50 +  if (url.pathname === "/api/v1/models/list") {
     51 +    return sendJson(response, 200, {
     52 +      ok: true,
     53 +      providers: {
     54 +        openai: { configured: Boolean(process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY), model: process.env.OPENAI_MODEL || "" },
     55 +        ollama: { configured: Boolean(process.env.OLLAMA_BASE_URL), model: process.env.OLLAMA_MODEL || "" }
     56 +      }
     57 +    });
     58 +  }
     59 +
     60 +  if (url.pathname === "/api/v1/inquiries/submit" && request.method === "POST") {
     61 +    const body = await readRequestJson(request);
     62 +    if (!body.name || !body.email || !body.message) {
     63 +      return sendJson(response, 400, { ok: false, error: "name, email, and message are required" });
     64 +    }
     65 +    return sendJson(response, 200, { ok: true, inquiry_id: crypto.randomUUID(), target_email: process.env.AIFRE
         D_CONTACT_EMAIL || "north3rnlight3rofficial@outlook.com" });
     66 +  }
     67 +
     68 +  if (url.pathname === "/api/v1/chat/ask") {
     69 +    return sendJson(response, 503, { ok: false, error: "Use Cloudflare Pages or configure provider calls in the
          deployed backend for chat." });
     70 +  }
     71 +
     72 +  return sendJson(response, 404, { ok: false, error: `unknown route: ${url.pathname}` });
     73 +}
     74 +
     75 +function staticPath(urlPath) {
     76 +  const decoded = decodeURIComponent(urlPath === "/" ? "/index.html" : urlPath);
     77 +  const resolved = path.resolve(siteRoot, `.${decoded}`);
     78 +  if (!resolved.startsWith(siteRoot)) return "";
     79 +  return resolved;
     83 +  try {
     84 +    const url = new URL(request.url || "/", `http://${request.headers.host || "localhost"}`);
     85 +    if (url.pathname.startsWith("/api/")) return routeApi(request, response, url);
     86 +
     87 +    const filePath = staticPath(url.pathname);
     88 +    if (!filePath || !existsSync(filePath)) {
     89 +      response.writeHead(404, { "content-type": "text/plain; charset=utf-8" });
     90 +      response.end("Not found");
     91 +      return;
     92 +    }

› how to get my api token secret
⚠ Heads up, you have less than 25% of your 5h limit left. Run /status for a breakdown.

• To get the Cloudflare API token for CLOUDFLARE_API_TOKEN:

  1. Open Cloudflare Dashboard: https://dash.cloudflare.com/profile/api-tokens
  2. Click Create Token.
  3. Use Custom token.
  4. Give it a name like AIFRED GitHub Pages Deploy.

  gh secret set CLOUDFLARE_API_TOKEN --repo kaeganscott26/AIFRED

  Paste the token when gh prompts for it.

  I already set CLOUDFLARE_ACCOUNT_ID in the GitHub repo. After CLOUDFLARE_API_TOKEN is set, push to main again or rerun


• I can handle the GitHub secret if I have the token value, but I may not be able to create a user API token through the
  account-scoped Cloudflare connector. I’m checking the Cloudflare API surface now; if token creation is not exposed
  here, I’ll use the connector to deploy directly and leave the GitHub secret step for the dashboard token.

         me}");
     21 +
     22 +    var tempRoot = Path.Combine(Path.GetTempPath(), "AIFRED-VST3-Setup-" + Guid.NewGuid().ToS
         tring("N"));

     24 +    Directory.CreateDirectory(extractedRoot);
     25 +
     26 +    try
     27 +    {
     28 +        using var archive = new ZipArchive(resource, ZipArchiveMode.Read);
     29 +        foreach (var entry in archive.Entries.Where(entry => entry.FullName.StartsWith(Plugin
         FolderName + "/", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)))
     30 +        {
     31 +            var destination = Path.GetFullPath(Path.Combine(extractedRoot, entry.FullName.Rep
         lace('/', Path.DirectorySeparatorChar)));
     32 +            if (!destination.StartsWith(Path.GetFullPath(extractedRoot), StringComparison.Ord
         inalIgnoreCase))
     33 +            {
     34 +                throw new InvalidOperationException("Installer payload contains an unsafe pat
         h.");
     35 +            }

     39 +                Directory.CreateDirectory(destination);
     40 +                continue;
     41 +            }
     42 +
     43 +            Directory.CreateDirectory(Path.GetDirectoryName(destination)!);
     44 +            entry.ExtractToFile(destination, overwrite: true);
     45 +        }
     46 +
     47 +        var sourcePlugin = Path.Combine(extractedRoot, PluginFolderName);
     48 +        if (!Directory.Exists(sourcePlugin))
     49 +        {
     50 +            throw new InvalidOperationException("Installer payload did not contain the VST3 b
         undle.");
     51 +        }
     52 +

     55 +        {
     56 +            Directory.Delete(targetPlugin, recursive: true);
     57 +        }
     58 +
     59 +        CopyDirectory(sourcePlugin, targetPlugin);
     60 +
     61 +        Console.WriteLine();
     62 +        Console.WriteLine("AIFRED installed.");
     63 +        Console.WriteLine("Open FL Studio, go to Plugin Manager, add or rescan this folder:")
         ;

     65 +        Console.WriteLine();

         r terminal with: --system");

     68 +    }

     76 +}

     83 +}

         ectories))
